<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хомяк.html>хомя́к</a> (17951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хомяк.html>хомя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xomják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хомяк.html>хомяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хомяк.html>хомяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хомяк.html>хомяко́в</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хомячо́к</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hamster (small, short-tailed European rodent)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> homepage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone's fanboy; narrow-minded follower (usually of a blogger or a virtual community)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хор.html>хор</a> (3545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">χορός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chorós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***хоромы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоромы.html>хоро́мы</a> (23158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хоромъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoromŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xormъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>храм</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xram</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоромы.html>хоро́мы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xorómy</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хор.html>хоро́м</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mansion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царский.html>ца́рские</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хоромы.html>хоро́мы</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cárskije <b>xorómy</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">royal residence/palace</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> palace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>них</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ра</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хоромы.html>хоро́мы</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nix ne kvartíra, a <b>xorómy</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">their flat/apartment is a real palace</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хоронить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>хорони́ть</a> (5331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xorniti</i>; compare its borrowed doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хранить.html>храни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xranítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>хорони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoronítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоронить.html>похорони́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схоронить.html>схорони́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bury, to inter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hide, to conceal, to lay away</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">погреба́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pogrebátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***хороший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a> (117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хорошь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xorošĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (13th century). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoróšyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">харо́шы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xaróšy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">харашы́цца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xarašýcca</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to boast, to swagger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Further etymology unclear; probably originally abbreviated from the -шь form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хоро́брый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoróbryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xorbrъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, hence cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́брый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xrábryj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">храбръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xrabrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoróšij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лу́чше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наилучший.html>наилу́чший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>good
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шим</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ком</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On byl <b>xoróšim</b> čelovékom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He was a <b>good</b> person.</span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1983</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuil_Marshak" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuil Marshak">Samuil Marshak</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:баллада.html>Балла́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:королевский.html>короле́вском</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́де</a></cite>  | <cite>Ballad of the King's Bread</cite> | , translation of <cite>The King’s Breakfast</cite> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._A._Milne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A. A. Milne">A. A. Milne</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>ска́жет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:тиран.html>тира́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумасброд.html>сумасбро́д</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́д</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Niktó ne skážet, búdto ja / Tirán i sumasbród, / Za tó, što k čáju ja ljubljú / <b>Xoróšij</b> butɛrbród/buterbród.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">“No one would say that I / Am a tyrant and madman, / For the fact that with my tea I like / A <b>good</b> bread-and-butter sandwich.”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>fine, nice</li>
<li>pretty, good-looking, handsome</li></ol>

***хотение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́ние</a> (30063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoténije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wish, desire, want, lust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щучий.html>щу́чьему</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́нию</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́нию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po ščúčʹjemu veléniju, po mojemú <b>xoténiju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the pike's behest and on my request (from a folk-tale)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хотеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́ть</a> (90)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хотѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xotěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xotěti</i> (Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">хотѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xotěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ща</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">htjeti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chcieć</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">chcieť</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xotétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захотеть.html>захоте́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to want, to desire</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> (246)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xotʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>although</li>
<li>even if</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xotʹ</span>)
</p>

<li>for example, even, you may, might as well</li></ol>

***хохол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохо́л</a> (16955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoxolъ</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chochoł</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chachoł</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">chochol</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохо́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoxól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохлы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохло́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хохлу́шка</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хохля́чка</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохолок.html>хохоло́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(birds)</i> crest, <i>(human hair)</i> topknot, tuft of hair</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Ukrainian, khokhol</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Originally the term was for Ukrainians, Belarusians and Zaporizhzhia Cossacks and also for simple people ("<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:князь.html>князья́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохло́в</a></i>..." A. Pushkin). The term was not always pejorative in Russia and is sometimes used by Ukrainians themselves in jest or ironically ("Українці мої! <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>Да́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бо́же</a> і щастя, і <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a>. Можна бути <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохло́м</a></i>, і <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> згіркне від <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> хлібина..." V. Baranov (Ukrainian writer)). There are proper names based on "<a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>хохо́л</a>" - e.g. <a href = vnd.unilang:хохол.html>Хохо́л</a>, Хохольский, Хохол-Тростянка, etc.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">topknot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуб.html>чуб</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чупрун</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čuprun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихо́р</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vixór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оселедец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oseledec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Ukrainian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">укр</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>offensive</i>), <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укроп.html>укро́п</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukróp</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>offensive, "dill"</i>), <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:украинец.html>украи́нец</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukraínec</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>neutral term</i>)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хохлушка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xoxluška</span>, <span class="ann-pos">noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***хохот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хот</a> (4368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>According to Vasmer, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoxotъ</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoxotati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to laugh loudly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xóxot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хота</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хоты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хотов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>laughter, roar, guffaw</li></ol>

***хохотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохота́ть</a> (2914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xoxotati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoxotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захохотать.html>захохота́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотнуть.html>хохотну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to laugh loudly, to laugh heartily, to roar with laughter, to guffaw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохота́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xoxotátʹ</b> do upádu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll with laughter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохота́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xoxotátʹ</b> do sljóz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to laugh until tears run</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежик.html>Ёжик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежи́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохо́чет</a></b>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:ежик.html>Ёжику</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вка</a> пипи́ську <a href = vnd.unilang:щекотать.html>щеко́чет</a>.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закончиться.html>зако́нчилась</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:гравий.html>гра́вий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошёл</a> —<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:ежик.html>Ёжик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> пипи́ськи <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jóžik po trávke bežít i <b>xoxóčet</b>,<br />Jóžiku trávka pipísʹku ščekóčet.<br />Trávka zakónčilasʹ, grávij pošól —<br />Jóžik domój bez pipísʹki prišól.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A hedgehog runs over grass and laughs,<br />The grass tickles his wienie.<br />But the grass has run out, and been followed by gravel —<br />The hedgehog had no wienie left by the time he got home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***хохотнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хохотнуть.html>хохотну́ть</a> (12514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотнуть.html>хохотну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xoxotnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хохотать.html>хохота́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to laugh loudly, to laugh heartily, to roar with laughter, to guffaw <i>(semelfactive)</i></li></ol>

***храбрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́брый</a> (6056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">храбръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xrabrŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xorbrъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Displaced the native East Slavic form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хоро́брый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoróbryj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́брый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xrábryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)храбре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)храбре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brave, courageous (strong in the face of fear)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бесстрашный.html>бесстра́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">besstrášnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отважный.html>отва́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otvážnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>сме́лый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smélyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***храм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>храм</a> (1987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">храмъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xramŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xormъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоромы.html>хоро́мы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xorómy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>храм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xram</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>хра́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>хра́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>хра́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>temple
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>храм</a></b> артеми́ды эфе́сской</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xram</b> Artemídy Efésskoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>Temple</b> of Artemis at Ephesus</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> church, cathedral <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a place of Christian worship that has an altar</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>храм</a></b> васи́лия <a href = vnd.unilang:блаженный.html>блаже́нного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xram</b> Vasílija Blažénnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saint_Basil%27s_Cathedral" class="extiw" title="w:Saint Basil | s Cathedral">Saint Basil's <b>Cathedral</b></a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shrine</li></ol>
